\newentry
\hypertarget{hvo22688}{}%
\headword{maasɪ}%
\hypertarget{hvo43702}{}%
\ipa{mààsɪ̀}%
\pos{v}%
%
%
\sensenr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo12438}{}%
\definition{to be earlier or already, Gh. Eng. ever}%
\lsgloss{earlier (be); already}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo33132}{}%
\vernacular{ɪ̀ kà máásɪ́ kààlɪ̀ bɛ̀lɛ̀ɛ́ dɪ̀ ǹ̩ wàà tùó.}%
\hypertarget{hvo33132}{}%
\modvernacular{ɪ̀ kà máá\-sɪ́ kàà\-lɪ̀ bɛ̀lɛ̀ɛ́ dɪ̀ ǹ̩ wàà tùó.}%
\hypertarget{hvo15168}{}%
\trs{The time you went to Gurumbele, I was not there.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo2936}{}%
\vernacular{ǹ̩ máásɪ́ bìgìsì tɪ̄ɛ̄ɪ̄ kéŋ tɪ̀ŋ bà kà jáʊ́.}%
\hypertarget{hvo2936}{}%
\modvernacular{ǹ̩ máá\-sɪ́ bì\-gìsì tɪ̄ɛ̄ɪ̄ kéŋ tɪ̀ŋ bà kà jáʊ́.}%
\hypertarget{hvo41437}{}%
\trs{I have already demonstrated to you how to do it.}%
\sensenr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo20279}{}%
\definition{to be enough, in satisfactory state, to be right amount or size}%
\lsgloss{enough; right; okay}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo24092}{}%
\vernacular{à máásɪ́ʊ́ kéŋ̀, tɪ́ brà jólīī.}%
\hypertarget{hvo24092}{}%
\modvernacular{à máá\-sɪ́ʊ́ kéŋ̀, tɪ́ brà jó\-līī.}%
\hypertarget{hvo22210}{}%
\trs{It is okay like that, stop pouring.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo32343}{}%
\vernacular{ʊ̀ máásɪ́ kpʊ̄ kɪ̀rɪ̀nsá wá àká ná bár pàrà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo32343}{}%
\modvernacular{ʊ̀ máá\-sɪ́ kpʊ̄ kɪ̀rɪ̀n\-sá wá à\-ká ná bár pà\-rà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo23832}{}%
\trs{He killed enough tsetse flies to get a chance to the farm.}%
\sensenr{3}%
\hypertarget{hvo19293}{}%
\definition{to fit, to be worthy}%
\lsgloss{fit; worthy}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo30082}{}%
\vernacular{nààtɔ́wá hámà, áwèmē kàá mààsɪ̀ ǹǹ nààsá?}%
\hypertarget{hvo30082}{}%
\modvernacular{nàà\-tɔ́\-wá há\-mà, á\-wèmē kàá màà\-sɪ̀ ǹǹ nàà\-sá?}%
\hypertarget{hvo18575}{}%
\trs{These sandals, which of them would fit my feet?}%
\sensenr{4}%
\hypertarget{hvo29191}{}%
\definition{to be equal, to make equal or even}%
\lsgloss{equal; even}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo13080}{}%
\vernacular{nɪ̀búlúmmò múŋ̀ wà māāsɪ̄ dɔ́ŋà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo13080}{}%
\modvernacular{nɪ̀bú\-lúmmò múŋ̀ wà māā\-sɪ̄ dɔ́\-ŋà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo28333}{}%
\trs{Human beings are not equal.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo19571}{}%
\vernacular{wʊ̀sá nɪ́ áfíá bɪ̀nsá máásɪ́ dɔ́ŋá rà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo19571}{}%
\modvernacular{wʊ̀sá nɪ́ á\-fíá bɪ̀n\-sá máá\-sɪ́ dɔ́\-ŋá rà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo2059}{}%
\trs{Wusa is as old as Afia.}%

\newentry
\homograph{1}%
\headword{maŋa}%
\hypertarget{hvo22317}{}%
\ipa{màŋà}%
\pos{v}%
\typecf{\hyperlink{hvo35284}{tugo}; \hyperlink{hvo21071}{tʃasɪ}}%
%
%
\sensenr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo18379}{}%
\definition{to beat, slap, strike, or hit}%
\lsgloss{beat; slap}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo22772}{}%
\vernacular{ʊ̀ máŋá dáá rá.}%
\hypertarget{hvo22772}{}%
\modvernacular{ʊ̀ má\-ŋá dáá rá.}%
\hypertarget{hvo31190}{}%
\trs{He fought someone.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo4087}{}%
\vernacular{bà máŋá dáá rá.}%
\hypertarget{hvo4087}{}%
\modvernacular{bà má\-ŋá dáá rá.}%
\hypertarget{hvo11081}{}%
\trs{They exchange blows.}%
\sensenr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo42034}{}%
\definition{to kick a football}%
\lsgloss{kick}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo12434}{}%
\vernacular{ʊ̀ máŋá à bɔ́ɔ̀l dʊ́ tókóró ní.}%
\hypertarget{hvo12434}{}%
\modvernacular{ʊ̀ má\-ŋá à bɔ́ɔ̀l dʊ́ tó\-kóró ní.}%
\hypertarget{hvo20684}{}%
\trs{He kicked the ball in the window.}%
\sensenr{3}%
\hypertarget{hvo33827}{}%
\definition{to cause a plant to change appearance, usually caused by drought stress}%
\lsgloss{change appearance (plant)}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo6930}{}%
\vernacular{hɪ̀ĺ tʃɪ́ŋɪ̀ã̄, à múró màŋà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo6930}{}%
\modvernacular{hɪ̀ĺ tʃɪ́\-ŋɪ̀ã̄, à mú\-ró mà\-ŋà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo39205}{}%
\trs{Due to drought, the rice changed appearance.}%

\begin{letter}{n}
\newentry
\hypertarget{hvo29052}{}%
\headword{n}%
\hypertarget{hvo7144}{}%
\ipa{n̩}%
\varblockopener{}%
\typevar{\hyperlink{hvo4702}{m}}, \typevar{\hyperlink{hvo26254}{ŋ}}%
\varblockcloser{}%
%
\synpos{pro}%
\hypertarget{hvo12920}{}%
\definition{first person singular pronoun}%
\lsgloss{I}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo12505}{}%
\vernacular{bàà jááʊ̄ dɪ́ ń̩ń̩ tʃélè.}%
\hypertarget{hvo12505}{}%
\modvernacular{bàà jááʊ̄ dɪ́ ń̩ń̩ tʃé\-lè.}%
\hypertarget{hvo5350}{}%
\trs{They are doing everything for me to fail.}%
%------------------------------
\newentry
\homograph{1}%
\headword{na}%
\hypertarget{hvo4389}{}%
\ipa{ná}%
\pos{v}%
%
%
\sensenr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo12135}{}%
\definition{to see}%
\lsgloss{see}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo31243}{}%
\vernacular{ǹ̩ ná dɪ̀ ʊ̀ʊ̀ wɪ́kpágɪ́ɛ̀ wíréó.}%
\hypertarget{hvo31243}{}%
\modvernacular{ǹ̩ ná dɪ̀ ʊ̀ʊ̀ wɪ́\-kpágɪ́ɛ̀ wí\-réó.}%
\hypertarget{hvo16468}{}%
\trs{I see that his behaviour are good.}%
\sensenr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo32359}{}%
\definition{to feel, to perceive}%
\lsgloss{feel; perceive}%

\hypertarget{hvo879}{}%
\trs{Dip your finger and taste it to see.}%

\lsgloss{caution}%

\begin{letter}{ŋm}

\newentry
\hypertarget{hvo40560}{}%
\headword{ŋma}%
\hypertarget{hvo10642}{}%
\ipa{ŋmá}%
%
%
\sensenr{1}%
\synpos{v}%
\hypertarget{hvo10653}{}%
\definition{to say, to speak}%
\lsgloss{say; speak}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo920}{}%
\vernacular{ʊ̀ ŋmá dɪ́ à bɔ́nɪ̃́ɛ̃́ nɪ́ ɪ̀ kàá wàʊ̄.}%
\hypertarget{hvo920}{}%
\modvernacular{ʊ̀ ŋmá dɪ́ à bɔ́\-nɪ̃́ɛ̃́ nɪ́ ɪ̀ kàá wàʊ̄.}%
\hypertarget{hvo13628}{}%
\trs{He said that you might come.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo14348}{}%
\vernacular{ŋ̩̀ ŋmājɛ̃̄ tɪ̀ɛ̀ ǹ̩ǹ̩ hã́ã̀ŋ dɪ́ ʊ́ tɔ́ŋà nàmɪ̃̀ã́.}%
\hypertarget{hvo14348}{}%
\modvernacular{ŋ̩̀ ŋmā\-jɛ̃̄ tɪ̀ɛ̀ ǹ̩ǹ̩ hã́ã̀ŋ dɪ́ ʊ́ tɔ́\-ŋà nà\-mɪ̃̀ã́.}%
\hypertarget{hvo30052}{}%
\trs{I told my wife to cook the meat.}%
\sensenr{2}%
\synpos{pv}%
\hypertarget{hvo11546}{}%
\definition{to want, desiderative mood particle that expresses an intention}%
\lsgloss{desiderative; want}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo16344}{}%

\definition{to aim at with a gun}%

{\startexample}%

\hypertarget{hvo41589}{}%

\hypertarget{hvo17445}{}%

\modvernacular{pɔ́ à dɪ̀à\-nʊ̃̀ã́, bʊ̃́ʊ̃́ŋ ná ǹ̩ dɪ̀ búú\-rè ń̩ kpá\-gà.}%

\hypertarget{hvo11691}{}%
\modvernacular{bà bʊ̃̀ʊ̃̀ŋ dɪ́\-gɪ́ɪ́\-máŋá bà kà kpá\-jɛ̀ɛ̀ pɔ́ bā tɪ̀n\-tɪ̀ŋ.}%

\trs{The clouds have turned reddish.}%

\lsgloss{ripe (be)}%

\homograph{1}%
\headword{sɔŋ}%
\hypertarget{hvo4822}{}%
\ipa{sɔ́ŋ̀}%
\pos{n}%
\varblockopener{}%
\typevar{\hyperlink{hvo38428}{sɔ\-sɔŋ}}%
\varblockcloser{}%
%
\sensenr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo11302}{}%
\definition{cool, cold}%
\lsgloss{cool; cold}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo19583}{}%
\vernacular{nɪ̀ɪ̀sɔ́ŋ káá nɪ̀ɪ̀nʊ́ŋ̀ ɪ̀ dɪ̀ búúrè?}%
\hypertarget{hvo19583}{}%
\modvernacular{nɪ̀ɪ̀sɔ́ŋ káá nɪ̀ɪ̀nʊ́ŋ̀ ɪ̀ dɪ̀ búú\-rè?}%
\hypertarget{hvo41818}{}%
\trs{Do you want cool or hot water? }%
\sensenr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo21578}{}%
\definition{fresh or wet}%
\lsgloss{fresh}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo6435}{}%
\vernacular{kùórù kùó kpáámá wá bɪ̄ kpàgà pààtʃàksɔ́ná.}%
\hypertarget{hvo6435}{}%
\modvernacular{kùó\-rù kùó kpáá\-má wá bɪ̄ kpà\-gà pàà\-tʃàksɔ́\-ná.}%
\hypertarget{hvo20482}{}%
\trs{The yams at the chief's farm do not have fresh leaves anymore.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo284}{}%
\vernacular{dààsɔ́ná wàá kɪ̀ŋ mɔ́sɪ́ dīŋ.}%
\hypertarget{hvo284}{}%
\modvernacular{dàà\-sɔ́\-ná wàá kɪ̀ŋ mɔ́\-sɪ́ dīŋ.}%
\hypertarget{hvo6203}{}%
\trs{Wet wood cannot catch fire.}%

\newentry
\hypertarget{hvo15251}{}%
\headword{sʊga}%
\hypertarget{hvo17390}{}%
\ipa{sʊ̀gà}%
%
%
\synpos{v}%
\hypertarget{hvo12551}{}%
\definition{to court, to seek another person's love or pay special attention to people to win their favour}%
\lsgloss{court}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo3485}{}%
\vernacular{ɲáʊ́ wàá kɪ̀n sʊ̀gà hã́ã̀ŋ.}%
\hypertarget{hvo3485}{}%
\modvernacular{ɲáʊ́ wàá kɪ̀n sʊ̀gà hã́ã̀ŋ.}%
\hypertarget{hvo19468}{}%
\trs{Poor people cannot court women.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo9163}{}%
\vernacular{bà já sʊ̀gà hã́ã́ná rá, à ná hã́dɪ́ɪ́ŋ kpà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo9163}{}%
\modvernacular{bà já sʊ̀gà hã́ã́\-ná rá, à ná hã́\-dɪ́ɪ́ŋ kpà.}%
\hypertarget{hvo7254}{}%
\trs{They court women in order to select the right one to marry.}%
\exnr{3}%
\hypertarget{hvo17882}{}%
\vernacular{kàlá káá būūrè ŋmã́ã́ŋʊ́ rá, ká ʊ̀ wà zɪ́má hã́ã́sʊ̄gɪ̄ɪ̄.}%
\hypertarget{hvo17882}{}%
\modvernacular{kà\-lá káá būū\-rè ŋmã́ã́\-ŋʊ́ rá, ká ʊ̀ wà zɪ́\-má hã́ã́\-sʊ̄\-gɪ̄ɪ̄.}%
\hypertarget{hvo1025}{}%
\trs{Kala loves Mangu, but he does not know how to court women.}%
\exnr{4}%
\hypertarget{hvo24282}{}%
\vernacular{dùsééléé káá sʊ̀gà dààbàŋtólúgú bá káálɪ̀ dáámúŋ.}%
\hypertarget{hvo24282}{}%
\modvernacular{dù\-séé\-léé káá sʊ̀gà dàà\-bàŋtó\-lúgú bá káá\-lɪ̀ dáá\-múŋ.}%
\hypertarget{hvo40739}{}%
\trs{People from Ducie go to court the people of the shrine since they wish to go to the initiation.}%

\newentry
\homograph{2}%
\headword{sʊ̃ʊ̃}%
\hypertarget{hvo22308}{}%
\ipa{sʊ̃̀ʊ̃̀}%
%
%
\synpos{v}%
\hypertarget{hvo31085}{}%
\definition{to be quiet, to order for quietness, as used when a child is crying or when pacify a quarrel}%
\lsgloss{quiet (be)}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo16928}{}%
\vernacular{tíí būōlīī, sʊ̃̀ʊ̃̀ ɪ̀ɪ̀ nʊ̃̀ã́, nárá káá tʃʊ́á dūō rō.}%
\hypertarget{hvo16928}{}%
\modvernacular{tíí būō\-līī, sʊ̃̀ʊ̃̀ ɪ̀ɪ̀ nʊ̃̀ã́, ná\-rá káá tʃʊ́á dūō rō.}%

\headword{tantama}%
\hypertarget{hvo6084}{}%
\ipa{tántàmā}%
%
%
\synpos{ideo}%
\hypertarget{hvo31909}{}%
\definition{a little, Gh. Eng. small-small}%
\lsgloss{little}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo27011}{}%
\vernacular{jáá tʊ́mà tántàmā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo27011}{}%
\modvernacular{jáá tʊ́\-mà tán\-tàmā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo14461}{}%
\trs{Let us work a little bit.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo19645}{}%
\vernacular{à báhɪ̃́ɛ̃̀ wà bráà nā tántàmā múŋ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo19645}{}%
\modvernacular{à bá\-hɪ̃́ɛ̃̀ wà bráà nā tán\-tàmā múŋ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo17395}{}%
\trs{The old man cannot see a little anymore.}%
\exnr{3}%
\hypertarget{hvo155}{}%
\vernacular{ʊ̀ʊ̀ nʊ̃́ã́ nɪ̄ɪ̄ rà tàńtàmá.}%
\hypertarget{hvo155}{}%
\modvernacular{ʊ̀ʊ̀ nʊ̃́ã́ nɪ̄ɪ̄ rà tà\-ńtàmá.}%
\hypertarget{hvo33832}{}%
\trs{He drinks water slowly.}%

\hypertarget{hvo29747}{}%

\newentry
\hypertarget{hvo40271}{}%
\headword{tesi}%
\hypertarget{hvo23298}{}%
\ipa{tésí}%
\pos{v}%
%
%
\sensenr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo26289}{}%
\definition{to crack and remove shea nuts from the shell}%
\lsgloss{remove (shea nut)}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo33628}{}%
\vernacular{tʃúónó ǹ̩ dɪ̀ tésí.}%
\hypertarget{hvo33628}{}%
\modvernacular{tʃúó\-nó ǹ̩ dɪ̀ té\-sí.}%
\hypertarget{hvo21932}{}%
\trs{I am cracking and removing shea nuts.}%
\typesyn{\hyperlink{hvo11210}{tʃɪagɪ}}%
\usage{rare}%
\sensenr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo23046}{}%
\definition{to hatch}%
\lsgloss{hatch}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo15796}{}%
\vernacular{à zál tésìō.}%
\hypertarget{hvo15796}{}%
\modvernacular{à zál té\-sìō.}%
\hypertarget{hvo8643}{}%
\trs{The fowl has hatched.}%

\hypertarget{hvo5765}{}%
\ipa{tùgò}%
\pos{v}%
\typecf{\hyperlink{hvo36238}{maŋa}; \hyperlink{hvo21071}{tʃasɪ}}%
%
%
\sensenr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo24739}{}%
\definition{to beat a person or an animal}%
\lsgloss{beat}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo4257}{}%
\vernacular{bà túgó dɔ́ŋā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo4257}{}%
\modvernacular{bà tú\-gó dɔ́\-ŋā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo43522}{}%
\trs{They fought each other.}%
\sensenr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo32834}{}%
\definition{to pound with sharp movements}%
\lsgloss{pound}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo27977}{}%
\vernacular{ʊ̀ʊ̀ túgò kàpálà rā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo27977}{}%
\modvernacular{ʊ̀ʊ̀ tú\-gò kà\-pálà rā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo17791}{}%
\trs{She pounds the fufu.}%

\hypertarget{hvo22992}{}%
\headword{tʊa}%
\hypertarget{hvo17853}{}%
\ipa{tʊ̀ɔ̀}%
\pos{v}%
%
%
\sensenr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo16817}{}%
\definition{to deny}%
\lsgloss{deny}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo11538}{}%
\vernacular{ʊ̀ tʊ́ɔ́ ɪ̀ɪ̀ wɪ́ŋmáhã́ tɪ̀n nā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo11538}{}%
\modvernacular{ʊ̀ tʊ́ɔ́ ɪ̀ɪ̀ wɪ́\-ŋmáhã́ tɪ̀n nā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo6108}{}%
\trs{He denied your words.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo10786}{}%
\vernacular{ʊ̀ʊ̀ ɲɪ́ná pɪ́ɛ́sʊ́ʊ̄ dɪ́ ʊ̀ wà káálɪ́ kùó, ʊ̀ tʊ̀à nʊ̃̀ã́.}%
\hypertarget{hvo10786}{}%
\modvernacular{ʊ̀ʊ̀ ɲɪ́\-ná pɪ́ɛ́\-sʊ́ʊ̄ dɪ́ ʊ̀ wà káá\-lɪ́ kùó, ʊ̀ tʊ̀à nʊ̃̀ã́.}%
\hypertarget{hvo19745}{}%
\trs{His father asked him whether he went to the farm, he denied having been there.}%

\hypertarget{hvo28734}{}%

\hypertarget{hvo4912}{}%
\trs{The room is bright.}%
\typeant{\hyperlink{hvo4243}{doŋii}}%

\hypertarget{hvo9132}{}%
\definition{to be clean, to be pure}%
\lsgloss{clean; pure}%

\hypertarget{hvo5905}{}%
\definition{to pay attention to, to keep track of, be careful}%
\lsgloss{pay attention to; careful (be)}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo771}{}%
\vernacular{tʃálásɪ́ nʊ̃́ʊ̃̀ à wɪ́ɛ́ wɪ́wíré.}%
\hypertarget{hvo771}{}%
\modvernacular{tʃá\-lásɪ́ nʊ̃́ʊ̃̀ à wɪ́ɛ́ wɪ́\-wíré.}%
\hypertarget{hvo26626}{}%
\trs{Pay attention and listen to the matter carefully.}%
\sensenr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo23201}{}%

\lsgloss{wait}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo6464}{}%

\hypertarget{hvo6464}{}%
\modvernacular{bà tʃá\-lásʊ̀ʊ̀ bá náɪ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo33577}{}%
\trs{They are waiting to see you.}%

\lsgloss{pound}%

\ipa{tʃɪ́ntʃɛ́rɪ́ɪ́}%
%
%
\synpos{n}%
\hypertarget{hvo8152}{}%
\definition{edge}%
\lsgloss{edge}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo44519}{}%
\vernacular{zʊ̀ʊ̀ ǹ̩ǹ̩ dɪ̀á, ǹ̩ǹ̩ kàrántɪ̀à tʃʊ́á à dɪ̀à tʃɪ́ntʃɛ́rɪ́ɪ́ nɪ́.}%
\hypertarget{hvo44519}{}%
\modvernacular{zʊ̀ʊ̀ ǹ̩ǹ̩ dɪ̀á, ǹ̩ǹ̩ kà\-rán\-tɪ̀à tʃʊ́á à dɪ̀à tʃɪ́n\-tʃɛ́\-rɪ́ɪ́ nɪ́.}%
\hypertarget{hvo38264}{}%
\trs{Go in the house, my cutlass is at the edge of my room, somewhere along a wall.}%
\plural{\textsl{tʃɪn\-tʃɛrɛ}}%

\hypertarget{hvo43738}{}%
\modvernacular{kà\-lá mã̀ã́ à\-nɪ́ ʊ̀ ɲɪ́\-ná sʊ́\-wá, ʊ̀ wɪ́ɛ́ tʃɔ̀gɔ̀mɪ̀.}%
\hypertarget{hvo27471}{}%
\trs{The mother and father of Kala died, his condition has changed to the worse.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo33038}{}%
\vernacular{m̀m̀ mòlbìé tʃɔ́gɔ́mɪ̃́jʊ̃́ʊ̃́, ǹ̩ wàá kɪ̀n bɪ̀ jàwà púpù.}%
\hypertarget{hvo33038}{}%
\modvernacular{m̀m̀ mòl\-bìé tʃɔ́\-gɔ́\-mɪ̃́\-jʊ̃́ʊ̃́, ǹ̩ wàá kɪ̀n bɪ̀ jà\-wà pú\-pù.}%
\hypertarget{hvo42088}{}%
\trs{My money situation has changed to the worse, I cannot afford to buy a motorbike any longer.}%

%------------------------------
\newentry
\hypertarget{hvo21820}{}%
\headword{tʃɔra}%
\hypertarget{hvo25116}{}%
\ipa{tʃɔ̀rà}%
%
%
\synpos{v}%
\hypertarget{hvo4008}{}%
\definition{for plants, to sprout after cutting}%
\lsgloss{sprout}%
{\startexample}%
\hypertarget{hvo10714}{}%
\vernacular{tɔ́má ká ŋmɛ́ná sūōŋ sã̀ã̀ tùtó, à súóŋ bɪ́ tʃɔ̀ráʊ̄.}%
\hypertarget{hvo10714}{}%
\modvernacular{tɔ́\-má ká ŋmɛ́\-ná sūōŋ sã̀ã̀ tù\-tó, à súóŋ bɪ́ tʃɔ̀ráʊ̄.}%

\definition{to thresh maize, or remove soil from a tuber}%
\lsgloss{remove; thresh}%
{\startexample}
\exnr{1}%
\hypertarget{hvo34301}{}%
\vernacular{námùnāā káá kɪ̀ŋ wʊ̀rà ɲámmɪ̃́ɛ̃́.}%
\hypertarget{hvo34301}{}%
\modvernacular{ná\-mùnāā káá kɪ̀ŋ wʊ̀rà ɲám\-mɪ̃́ɛ̃́.}%
\hypertarget{hvo23217}{}%
\trs{Everyone can thresh maize.}%
\exnr{2}%
\hypertarget{hvo37259}{}%
\vernacular{wʊ̀rà kpáámá háglɪ́ɪ́ tā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo37259}{}%
\modvernacular{wʊ̀rà kpáá\-má hág\-lɪ́ɪ́ tā.}%
\hypertarget{hvo25187}{}%
\trs{Remove the sand from the yams.}%
